1 - paradox

frequecy : 4

S.N.: 1/1

  • n. an idea that, despite sound (or apparently sound) reasoning from acceptable premises, leads to a conclusion that seems senseless, logically unacceptable, or self-contradictory
  • n.反论，悖论； 似非而是的论点； 自相矛盾的人或事； [物]佯谬
  • n. 悖论，自相矛盾的话
  • 矛盾\nn. 似非而是的隽语,自相矛盾的话
